<div id="review_18765730" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/18765730" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/18765730?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Any romance fan, but especially a must read for Kleypas fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=lisa-kleypas">lisa-kleypas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2011_reads">2011_reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer18765730" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9467991054806258955">This won't be much of a review because I'm dying to get back to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4066312.Smooth_Talking_Stranger__Travises___3_' title='Smooth Talking Stranger (Travises, #3) by Lisa Kleypas' rel='nofollow noopener'>Smooth Talking Stranger</a> (which I already started). Just some of my thoughts...<br/><br/>Hardy...Hardy...<i>Hardy</i>! God, how I adored this character (and his 'mink' hair--I think LK went a <i>little</i> overboard on that description)! I love all the good, and the wee bit of bad, in Hardy. I love his charming side, his teasing side, his sexy side, his compassionate side, <i>and</i> his roguish side. What a perceptive, lovable, blue-eyed scamp! I was a bit worrie</span>
  <span id="freeText9467991054806258955" style="display:none">This won't be much of a review because I'm dying to get back to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4066312.Smooth_Talking_Stranger__Travises___3_" title="Smooth Talking Stranger (Travises, #3) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Smooth Talking Stranger</a> (which I already started). Just some of my thoughts...<br><br>Hardy...Hardy...<i>Hardy</i>! God, how I adored this character (and his 'mink' hair--I think LK went a <i>little</i> overboard on that description)! I love all the good, and the wee bit of bad, in Hardy. I love his charming side, his teasing side, his sexy side, his compassionate side, <i>and</i> his roguish side. What a perceptive, lovable, blue-eyed scamp! I was a bit worried about him at first, thinking he might be hung up on Liberty (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/306364.Sugar_Daddy__Travises___1_" title="Sugar Daddy (Travises, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Sugar Daddy</a>), and was relieved to see that wasn't the case, that he had moved on and was ready for someone to enter his life. Loved the chemistry he had with Haven, and was so, sooo relieved that Haven stood up to her family and fought for what she wanted. I loved these two together, and thought if anyone could restore Haven's confidence in herself and help her move forward, it would be Hardy.<br><br><i>Hardy...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=hardy.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379762214i/208878._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book was almost too hard to read at first. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The scenes of domestic violence between Haven and her husband Nick...wow...I kept wondering when Haven was finally going to say enough is enough. And LK nearly pushed <i>me</i> to the breaking point--I couldn't take much more of Nick and wanted to rip his throat out! I thought LK did an excellent job though with these scenes and the therapy scenes describing the kind of personality disorder that Nick had--some frightening, and unfortunately all to true-to-life stuff there. I was just glad that Haven was able to get out alive. I have to admit that I <i>was</i> a bit disappointed that Haven's brothers Gage, Jack and Joe didn't give him the woopin' he deserved, though. But I guess it was meant to be that Hardy took care of that! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I loved Hardy's rags-to-riches story. I loved his drive and ambition. I loved how he took care of his family <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ (although I was a bit surprised that he paid his father to stay away from the family--I wouldn't have given him a dime). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> The scene near the end where Hardy got a call from his family, which sort of sent him into a tailspin thinking he wasn't good enough for Haven? It just about broke my heart. But I <i>loved</i> how Haven had no doubts about Hardy and was ready to fight for her man!<br><br>The previous book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/306364.Sugar_Daddy__Travises___1_" title="Sugar Daddy (Travises, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Sugar Daddy</a>, was more of an epic soap opera, but provided plenty of background about the character of Hardy and where he came from. I think it's a <i>must</i> to read that book first in order to get the full effect of "Blue-Eyed Devil". This one was much more like a standard romance (and oh yeah, Haven and Hardy's bedroom scenes were <i>hot</i>)! I didn't mind that the story was told from Haven's POV, but I still wished for a chapter (or two) of Hardy's POV...:(<br><br>To sum up, a verrrry satisfying read. Hardy and Haven may be my favorite couple and their story my favorite contemporary read of the year. 5 Texas-big stars!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9467991054806258955" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1236230772" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1236230772" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1236230772?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1236230772" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3726473940572918666"><b>5 STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584143934i/29103271._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Those blue eyes glinted with uncivilized suggestion. A faint smile was tucked in the corner of his wide mouth. Definitely wouldn't want to be alone in a room with that guy, I thought. His gaze moved downward in lazy inspection, returned to my face, and he gave me one of those respectful nods that Texan men had raised to an art form.</blockquote>
</b><br/>Wow. This book really caught me off-guard. I was not expecting the intensity to be quite so high. I really had trouble putting it down. As a whole I'm rati</span>
  <span id="freeText3726473940572918666" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584143934i/29103271._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Those blue eyes glinted with uncivilized suggestion. A faint smile was tucked in the corner of his wide mouth. Definitely wouldn't want to be alone in a room with that guy, I thought. His gaze moved downward in lazy inspection, returned to my face, and he gave me one of those respectful nods that Texan men had raised to an art form.</blockquote>
</b><br>Wow. This book really caught me off-guard. I was not expecting the intensity to be quite so high. I really had trouble putting it down. As a whole I'm rating it a five, but that does not mean that there weren't things I didn't like. The most prominent being Haven, herself. She was the youngest child of four, and the only girl. Which is exactly my own background. So I can say with experience, that I know how it feels to be this overlooked, whiney sibling. But honestly I found Haven's character just a little bit to0 immature and almost bratty when she dealt with her family. I don't know why I felt the need to say that in the review, but there it is. <br><br>Otherwise I loved the book. I loved Hardy! I would have liked more time with these two. The story was too complicated though to focus only on merely their relationship. In fact, if you are thinking of reading this, you really need to read the first book in the series before you can truly understand our boy, Hardy Cates. <br><br>I can easily say, I am loving this series, and looking forward to the next Travis!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3726473940572918666" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/652194411?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2013</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer652194411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15578659989862086732">Sometimes you come across a book that leaves you speechless. It leaves you empty upon finishing it because it was such a pleasure reading it.<br/><br/>THIS WAS ONE OF THOSE BOOKS!<br/><br/>Blue-Eyed Devil was my first LK novel and it left me wondering, agonizing, why it took me so damn long to read her work. She is a brilliant writer. BRILLIANT.<br/>She tells a story so evocatively, so intelligently it makes you wonder about other books you've read. I was amazed by LK's ability to use such descriptive language and witty</span>
  <span id="freeText15578659989862086732" style="display:none">Sometimes you come across a book that leaves you speechless. It leaves you empty upon finishing it because it was such a pleasure reading it.<br /><br />THIS WAS ONE OF THOSE BOOKS!<br /><br />Blue-Eyed Devil was my first LK novel and it left me wondering, agonizing, why it took me so damn long to read her work. She is a brilliant writer. BRILLIANT.<br />She tells a story so evocatively, so intelligently it makes you wonder about other books you've read. I was amazed by LK's ability to use such descriptive language and witty dialogue in her writing.<br /><br />And for something so smartly written it was equally engrossing. Many people have read this book so I won't go into the plot, but I absolutely fell in love with it and the characters.<br /><br />The first half of the book dedicated to Haven's disaster of a marriage to an abusive brute was very frightening. The trauma and eventual erosion of Haven's self worth was felt so acutely by me it was scary. The breakdown of a marriage is something, but the breakdown of one's spirit in the face of the ultimate betrayal was something else entirely.<br /><br />I couldn't believe the experience Haven went through, always doubting her self and her mind. Nick was the definition of monster. He was brutal and savage in his treatment of her and I was hoping against everything she'd get out.<br /><br />The second half of the book we saw Haven healing and leaning on her family for support. That same support from Gabe and Jack even Liberty was astounding. Despite being cut off from them they were there when it counted and I loved seeing that.<br /><br />Now on to the good stuff! Hardy, Hardy, Hardy!!! The alpha male accentuated by being raised a Texan was incredible! He was the man of men, the alpha of the pack and I LOVED HIM.<br />The opening scene at Gabe's and Liberty's wedding was so sensually raw and hot, it set a precident for both of them that finally came to fruition years later.<br /><br />I loved the excrutiating sexual chemistry, the no-holds-barred attitude of Hardy and their eventual coming together. Hardy's characterization was spot on as the blue-collar kid from the wrong side of the tracks that fed off ambition. He was the perfect man for Haven and she was the perfect woman for him.<br /><br />I can't express how much I loved this book! It had all the elements of a wonderful story without the plot being riddled with useless filler. That is the benchmark of a fabulous writer. LOVED IT!!<br />Looking forward to the rest of this series and LK's other works!<br /><br />GENRE: Contemporary Romance<br />STEAM: High<br />POV: 1st person, Haven<br />CLIFFY: HEA with Jack's story for the next book</span>
  <a data-text-id="15578659989862086732" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_40582388" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/40582388" />
    <a title="Miss Kim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/925549-miss-kim"><img alt="Miss Kim" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369060240p2/925549.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/40582388?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miss Kim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miss Kim" href="/user/show/925549-miss-kim">Miss Kim</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">any CR fan</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Miss Kim by: </span>
      Teryl, continuation of a series
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/925549-miss-kim?shelf=2009">2009</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/925549-miss-kim?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer40582388" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2150530817731240912"><i>Blue Eyed Devi</i>l was an awesome follow up to <i>Sugar Daddy</i>. I was disappointed that Hardy didn’t end up with Liberty in that one, especially after all of the background we get on him. Then he just leaves town, and comes back to pull a total a-hole move in order to get Liberty back. <br/>In BED, we get to know Haven, the youngest daughter of the Sugar Daddy, Churchill. She first meets Hardy at Liberty and Gage’s wedding and they have the classic moment. “Their eyes meet across a crowded room….causing hea</span>
  <span id="freeText2150530817731240912" style="display:none"><i>Blue Eyed Devi</i>l was an awesome follow up to <i>Sugar Daddy</i>. I was disappointed that Hardy didn’t end up with Liberty in that one, especially after all of the background we get on him. Then he just leaves town, and comes back to pull a total a-hole move in order to get Liberty back. <br />In BED, we get to know Haven, the youngest daughter of the Sugar Daddy, Churchill. She first meets Hardy at Liberty and Gage’s wedding and they have the classic moment. “Their eyes meet across a crowded room….causing heart palpitations and damp undergarments”. Later she follows a guy who she thinks is her boyfriend into a wine closet and makes out with him, and gets pretty darn close to closing the deal. Suddenly she realizes its not her boyfriend, Nick, but Hardy instead. I do find it hard to believe you can be making out heavily with someone and not know its not your intimate partner. Not by his smell, the way he kisses, the size of certain <i>things</i>? But it’s a novel, and I chose to believe it at this moment, anyway. She leaves the closet and doesn’t see him for a few years.<br />She marries, Nick, a total a-hole who abuses her progressively until he ends up beating the shit out of her and then eventually raping her and leaving her to die. It’s pretty brutal.<br />She gets away from Nick and reconnects with her family, and ends up running into Hardy again. He remembers her too, and starts to pursue. He has no idea what she’s been through. She’s very attracted to him, but doesn’t want a relationship. She’s trying to change herself, and not let her brothers, father, boss, run her life and make decisions for her. <br />I felt Haven grew throughout the book, and of course fell for Hardy big time. His eyes are mentioned so much, I started to picture his eyes like young Paul Newman. Her ex shows up the picture again creating added strain and danger. I don't want to give anything else away. I was happy with the HEA, and I know you will be too.<br /><br /><b>Warning: There is spousal abuse, and a rape scene that may be uncomfortable for some readers.</b><br /><br /><br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3299611387" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11615939050889841238">I am not even sure if I had previously read this one. I think I did years ago, before Goodreads maybe 🤷‍♀️<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1587914858i/29360856._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I have never been to Texas. I would love to visit sometime. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>... friendship was a lot more dependable, not to mention long-lasting, than love.</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>We met Hardy in the first book. I liked him but he was a bit of a con-artist. Seemed to be out for himself. <br/><br/><blockquote>

  <span id="freeText11615939050889841238" style="display:none">I am not even sure if I had previously read this one. He wasn't really a jackass ... much as he sorted of wanted folks to think he was.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1587914858i/29360859._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nice to catch up with the folks from the previous book and meet those in future books ... the next one sound familiar too but it's marked as unread so, we shall see!!<br><br><blockquote>

<div id="review_537547578" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537547578" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537547578?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781597378635" href="/book/show/7174378-blue-eyed-devil">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-series">cont-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=heroine-drove-me-batty">heroine-drove-me-batty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=if-this-guy-was-real">if-this-guy-was-real</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=wee-bit-dark">wee-bit-dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cranky-hero">cranky-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=there-will-be-blood">there-will-be-blood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=millionaire-billionaire-hero">millionaire-billionaire-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=douchewaffles-galore">douchewaffles-galore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537547578" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1901425539618057118"><b>Hardy...a <i>Devil???</i></b><br/><br/>It's not too often that you come across a contemporary romance author that can write a timeless book. Now, 2008 probably doesn't seem that long ago, but you would be surprised how quickly a book can seem out of date. Terminology, slang and modern technology changes quickly, daily even. I know in my own experience that my teen boys seem to even speak a different language to me. I've even had to translate hand-written notes for workmates because the cursive has changed so much in</span>
  <span id="freeText1901425539618057118" style="display:none"><b>Hardy...a <i>Devil???</i></b><br /><br />It's not too often that you come across a contemporary romance author that can write a timeless book. Now, 2008 probably doesn't seem that long ago, but you would be surprised how quickly a book can seem out of date. Terminology, slang and modern technology changes quickly, daily even. I know in my own experience that my teen boys seem to even speak a different language to me. I've even had to translate hand-written notes for workmates because the cursive has changed so much in the twenty years between our schooling. Sure, some of the things we witness in <i>Blue-Eyed Devil</i> seem a little behind the times, but I think it had more to do with the characters than the times.<br /><br />Haven was a bloody idiot. OK, that's probably a little harsh. I just found myself completely frustrated with her when she allowed herself to be mentally and physically abused. I know, I know, bad Sassy for being so judgemental and narrow-minded. I just can't see myself EVER putting up with what she dealt with and it wasn't just at the hands of her despicable husband. I could write a list and a ten-page essay on all the douchewaffles she's faced in her life. I guess those little hits to the self-esteem in your childhood really do leave you with permanent scars.<br /><br />I have to admit that this was a LOT more emotional than I expected. I kind of wish I'd known how much before I decided to listen to the audio on public transport. No sunglasses, a train carriage full of blokes...it was not a pretty sight. There were plenty of highs and lows that kept me a bit of an emotional wreck through this one. Mind you, it was never OTT or made me want to discontinue. It was just a wee bit confronting. I felt like I was there, with my hands tied behind my back and my screams of warning falling on deaf ears. I sometimes hate feeling helpless...I get way too "into" my books.<br /><br />Now, the narrator, she does a very...ah...Southern accent with a twist (quoting Wikipedia). I almost needed an interpreter at times and even had to replay it to catch the meaning. As I'm not from Texas or even America, it took a little more effort listening. Please excuse my ignorance if I got that all wrong. Let's just say that I knew it was a Southern accent, I'm just guessing that it was Texan.<br /><br />After all that, the highlight for me was Hardy Cates. Oh boy, he made my heart flutter. A bad boy who was just waiting for the right woman to come into his life. Sure, he had his fun until she was ready, but boy does he use his experience well. Honestly, considering the characters in his midst, he was far from a devil. I think this story should have been called - Blue-Eyed...Sexy, Bossy, Dirty-talking, Bad Boy, with a heart of gold and a magic touch. But, obviously, that's a wee bit too long.<br /><br /><i>Lisa Kleypas</i> is a bit of a legend. I am a HUGE fan of her historical romances but her contemporary romances are nothing to laugh at. If I had my way, she would write morning, noon and night and alternate between the two. Pretty please with sugar on the top.<br /><br />I highly recommend <i>Blue-Eyed Devil</i> and will definitely be going on in the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1901425539618057118" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_405974524" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/405974524" />
    <a title="Ronyell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell"><img alt="Ronyell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1506581787p2/1169488.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/405974524?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ronyell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ronyell" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell">Ronyell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Lisa Kleypas fans!!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=lisa-kleypas">lisa-kleypas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=my-blog-reviews">my-blog-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=sexy-good-girl-heroine">sexy-good-girl-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=adult-book">adult-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=aar-top-100-romance-books-2010">aar-top-100-romance-books-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=sexy-bad-boy-hero">sexy-bad-boy-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=ronyell-s-epinions-reviews">ronyell-s-epinions-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=1st-person-pov">1st-person-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer405974524" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4691039561015543754">Wow! Can I officially say that “Blue-Eyed Devil” by Lisa Kleypas has now become one of my top contemporary romance novels of all time next to “Kiss An Angel?” “Blue-Eyed Devil” is the second book in Lisa Kleypas popular “Travises” series and this time, it stars the sister in the family, Haven Travis and the former bad-boy, Hardy Cates! “Blue-Eyed Devil” is a truly mesmerizing book that has drama, secrets and forbidden love rolled into one novel!<br/><br/>Haven Travis is the only sister in the famous and f</span>
  <span id="freeText4691039561015543754" style="display:none">Wow! Can I officially say that “Blue-Eyed Devil” by Lisa Kleypas has now become one of my top contemporary romance novels of all time next to “Kiss An Angel?” “Blue-Eyed Devil” is the second book in Lisa Kleypas popular “Travises” series and this time, it stars the sister in the family, Haven Travis and the former bad-boy, Hardy Cates! “Blue-Eyed Devil” is a truly mesmerizing book that has drama, secrets and forbidden love rolled into one novel!<br><br>Haven Travis is the only sister in the famous and filthy rich Travis family and she is known to have a mind of her own. However, when Haven ends up marrying a man named Nick who she believed was her true love only to discover too late about his abusive ways, she believes that she may never find true love ever again. However years later, Haven meets Hardy Cates, her sister in law Liberty’s former love interest and enemy of her family and she will soon discover that not only does she start developing feelings for him, but she will soon uncover his dark past that will change her world forever.<br><br>Oh my goodness! This book really set my heart up in flames! “Blue-Eyed Devil” is certainly a huge improvement from the first book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/306364.Sugar_Daddy__Travises___1_" title="Sugar Daddy (Travises, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Sugar Daddy</a> as we get to learn more about the characters in this book (especially about Haven Travis!) Lisa Kleypas has done a brilliant job at developing a story that was quite unusual for any romance novel, but was still able to produce enough drama and romance that really made my heart flutter! What I mean by how this novel was quite unusual for a romance novel is that the story starts off with Haven being abused by her former husband Nick and this was the first romance novel that I had read that dealt with the subject matter of domestic abuse and it really made this story much more relatable to any reader who had also suffered through domestic abuse. I also loved the fact that Lisa Kleypas provided facts and helpful websites that would help the reader really understand the nature of domestic abuse and how to deal with them, which really helped me understand more about domestic violence. Now, onto the characters of this book! Haven Travis was just an amazing heroine throughout this book as she had to go through domestic abuse caused by her former husband and for awhile, she could not trust anyone with her issues and was afraid to get close to any man she had contact with. I actually found myself sympathizing so much with Haven’s situation as domestic abuse happens so much in real life and I was hoping throughout this story that she would find someone who can truly understand the horror she been through and be able to heal her pain. I also loved the way that Lisa Kleypas made Haven Travis into a strong and independent woman as she may have suffered through a terrible ordeal, but she still tries to move on with her life. Now, I am going to start getting all flirty whenever I am talking about Hardy Cates, the hero of the story, since he has become one of my most favorite romance heroes of all time! Hardy Cates has come a long way from the first book “Sugar Daddy” as he was Liberty’s former love interest and had become an enemy of the Travis family after his stunt in “Sugar Daddy.” However, Hardy Cates was probably the best character in this book as he may be the dangerous and sexy bad-boy that people would warn you to not get near, but he truly shows how much he cared about Haven and how he tries to help her through the ordeal she went through. Also, it would not hurt to mention that the fact that Hardy Cates is muscular, large and sexy all around just really makes me feel all giddy inside!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389902i/751286.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="Sexy Cowboy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Since this novel discusses about domestic abuse and gives vivid detail about the abuse that Haven has suffered at the hands of her former husband, some readers who do not like reading about such subject matter might feel a bit uncomfortable reading this novel and they might want to see if they can handle such subject matter before reading this book. Also, this book has many scenes that detail explicit sex and they might want to skim over these sex scenes if they feel uncomfortable about them.<br><br>Overall, “Blue-Eyed Devil” is definitely one romance novel that you have to check out and I am definitely looking forward to the next book in the “Travis” series <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4066312.Smooth_Talking_Stranger__Travises___3_" title="Smooth Talking Stranger (Travises, #3) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Smooth Talking Stranger</a>! <br><br><b>Review is also on: <a href="http://rabbitearsbookblog.blogspot.com/2012/09/blue-eyed-devil-by-lisa-kleypas.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabbit Ears Book Blog</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4691039561015543754" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1589864929?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacob Proffitt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacob Proffitt" href="/user/show/1331641-jacob-proffitt">Jacob Proffitt</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1589864929" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13308528222539098649">I've been busy enough lately that my time here on GoodReads has dwindled. As a consequence, I'm afraid I'm falling behind in my reviews (and yes, being busy cuts into my reading time, too, but not at the same rate—I have priorities, thankyouverymuch). So I finished this almost a week ago and the details have gone a bit fuzzy. I'll do my best, but now you know not to expect my best work...<br/> <br/>This review will have a spoiler for the first quarter or so of the book. It's not major (you can probably as</span>
  <span id="freeText13308528222539098649" style="display:none">I've been busy enough lately that my time here on GoodReads has dwindled. As a consequence, I'm afraid I'm falling behind in my reviews (and yes, being busy cuts into my reading time, too, but not at the same rate—I have priorities, thankyouverymuch). So I finished this almost a week ago and the details have gone a bit fuzzy. I'll do my best, but now you know not to expect my best work...<br /> <br />This review will have a spoiler for the first quarter or so of the book. It's not major (you can probably assume the trajectory without confirming the destination), but it is key to the plot. I don't mind giving readers a heads-up about it, but it's only fair to indicate it's coming for those who want to remain completely unspoiled going in.<br /><br />I had a terrible time with the first part of this. I knew from the cover copy that Haven was headed for a rough time with her husband and the book lived up to that expectation. I know it's sexist, but I've always had a terribly hard time with violence against women. I don't care, it's just fundamentally <em>different</em>, at least in my emotional landscape. To Kleypas's credit, she treats it with the seriousness it deserves by both staying with Haven throughout, including a rape, and by giving it all the drama it deserves and not an iota more. In other words, she stuck to the essentials and left the events (and their aftermath) to speak for themselves.<br /><br />So I was beyond elated when Haven finally got out. And even more so that she had people she could rely on to take care of her and protect her at her most vulnerable. And yes, it was <em>awesome</em> to see Gage again and the kind of man we knew he was. That feeling was reinforced by Haven knowing she could throw an emergency line to him and <em>know</em>, fundamentally, that he'd catch it.<br /><br />I was even more elated when Hardy showed up. I'd already lost my heart to him in the first book and was disappointed when he blew it with Liberty. This was so much better, though, as it becomes clear how very much he needs Haven even as we know that she needs him. It was fantastic to see him learn and grow from the man for whom love wasn't enough to the one who knew it was everything. Watching them grow together in the teeth of the rest of the Travis clan was excellent. As nice was seeing Haven's father from her viewpoint as opposed to Liberty's. It was a more complete perspective of that family dynamic and very illustrative of why they are where they are (with the loyalty but essential disconnection we see them in as the series starts).<br /><br />I had a bit of a harder time with Haven. She was so fragile and my heart ached for her, but that's an uncomfortable connection to a character, for me. It was a treat to see her grow strong. And fun to see her connect with Hardy. So it was very rewarding in the end.<br /><br />So the beginning drags a near four-star down. A lot, given how much that kind of thing is hard for me to tolerate. But Hardy pulls that back up leaving this a shaky, but appreciated, four stars.<br /><br /><strong>A note about Steamy</strong>: There are a couple explicit sex scenes, so the middle of my steam tolerance. And no, I'm not counting the rape. Kleypas takes a risk, here, as Hardy is all-alpha and sex play often includes elements of pursuit, capture, and dominance. And no, I'm not talking anything like S&amp;M or actual dom/sub here (i.e. nothing extraordinary, IMO). Just that Hardy is very forceful. Kleypas makes it work because while forceful, it's never even a little bit actual force. Showing that difference almost elevated this an extra star for me both because it is a hard thing to do and because she pulled it off so well. And for the record, I liked it even more when Haven was comfortable enough to turn it around and we got to see that Hardy was one of those excellent men who is perfectly capable of extending trust by forfeiting control when appropriate, in turn.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13308528222539098649" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_204066651" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/204066651" />
    <a title="Wendy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4485620-wendy"><img alt="Wendy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1332210853p2/4485620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/204066651?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy" href="/user/show/4485620-wendy">Wendy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer204066651" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1799782483598179589">What can I say? I've been sucked in, into the wonderful world of the pure bliss that LK has created. Alpha males that are just too good to be true and wonderful heroines. <br/><br/>This is my favorite, so far. Hardy you are a gem and you have found a beautiful heroine in Haven, who is such a sweetheart. <br/><br/>A special thanks to Karla, for providing this wonderful image of Hardy, that is just sublime. Thank you my friend, it really enhanced my reading experience. *waggles eyebrows*<br/><br/>Hardy Cates<br/><br/><a href='http://s1137.photobucket.com/albums/n517/winiguez/?action=view&current=Hardy.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379767122i/253756.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Thanks again Ka</span>
  <span id="freeText1799782483598179589" style="display:none">What can I say? I've been sucked in, into the wonderful world of the pure bliss that LK has created. Alpha males that are just too good to be true and wonderful heroines. <br><br>This is my favorite, so far. Hardy you are a gem and you have found a beautiful heroine in Haven, who is such a sweetheart. <br><br>A special thanks to Karla, for providing this wonderful image of Hardy, that is just sublime. Thank you my friend, it really enhanced my reading experience. *waggles eyebrows*<br><br>Hardy Cates<br><br><a href="http://s1137.photobucket.com/albums/n517/winiguez/?action=view&amp;current=Hardy.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Thanks again Karla, for letting me borrow your husband's pic! *giggles*<br><br>All in all this is a series, that has me besotted! Love it!<br></span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1919549980" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1919549980" />
    <a title="Irene Sim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31914348-irene-sim"><img alt="Irene Sim" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565617599p2/31914348.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1919549980?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Irene Sim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Irene Sim" href="/user/show/31914348-irene-sim">Irene Sim</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780812551839" href="/book/show/7113370-blue-eyed-devil">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31914348-irene-sim?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31914348-irene-sim?shelf=2017-read">2017-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31914348-irene-sim?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1919549980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15015339001313393051">The second time reading this story I enjoyed it even more. Somehow I noticed more details about the two protagonists, Hardy and Haven, that I missed the first time. <br/><br/>This story is about two people who don't know their designated place in life, so they drift wherever the wind takes them, persuing random avenues and finally finding their place in it's other's arms.<br/>Hardy Cates is for me (and I guess for whichever read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/306364.Sugar_Daddy__Travises___1_' title='Sugar Daddy (Travises, #1) by Lisa Kleypas' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sugar Daddy</a>) a repressed desire. He may acted like an asshole in the end of that b</span>
  <span id="freeText15015339001313393051" style="display:none">The second time reading this story I enjoyed it even more. Somehow I noticed more details about the two protagonists, Hardy and Haven, that I missed the first time. <br /><br />This story is about two people who don't know their designated place in life, so they drift wherever the wind takes them, persuing random avenues and finally finding their place in it's other's arms.<br />Hardy Cates is for me (and I guess for whichever read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/306364.Sugar_Daddy__Travises___1_" title="Sugar Daddy (Travises, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Sugar Daddy</a>) a repressed desire. He may acted like an asshole in the end of that book but I deffinitely wanted a HEA for him. Maybe Liberty wasn't his destiny but Haven surely is. <br /><br />What did the trick for me was the first scene of them in the wine cellar. This intimate meeting of them, without knowing each other, extricated any doupts I might have about Hardy's intentions or emotions for Haven, after he learned her name and who her family is. <br /><br />Their journey to each other isn't an easy one, Haven has made some bad choices in her life for which she paid in tears and blood, but I think it was necessary for her to become the strong woman she is in the end of the book.<br /><br />In the other hand, we witness Hardy becoming as uncertain about himself as any man can be when he finaly finds the person that matters the most in his life, and that weakness made him even more perfect for me.<br /><br />This series is so far great, Lisa Kleypa's writing is impecable as always, drawing all kind of emotions from the reader and if you love contemporary romance then these books is a must-read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15015339001313393051" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VObdK112kDjGJ+UzHJM4IhgFTb8yVOu+gpQKMGUiEZOyiaJvgi+ZectsCPm7OIk4fyLU6kuDeZUMUdtl52t8Tg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/wYBc8rcGdeTTIq7QYoBH57uUjal7beVneghxTWNzDIZaX43FYUQlp4HZ3HmIbAF+cnLY9w6Jb4TLfCQt8Sh7w==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
